About Me

I am a software engineer focused on building robust, scalable backend systems and seamless user interfaces. My approach marries technical precision with a clean, minimalist aesthetic.

With a strong foundation in systems architecture, I prioritize performance, maintainability, and elegant problem-solving. I view coding not just as typing instructions, but as crafting durable digital infrastructure.

When I'm not optimizing queries or refactoring legacy code, you can find me exploring new language paradigms or contributing to open-source tooling.
